        <script type="text/javascript">

            function pageLoad() {
                $(function () {
                    $(document).tooltip({
                        items: "img[alt], [title]",
                        hide: { effect: "fadeOut", duration: 5 },
                        content: function () {
                            var element = $(this);
                            if (element.is("[title]")) {
                                return element.attr("title");
                            }
                            if (element.is("img")) {
                                return element.attr("alt");
                            }
                        }
                    });
                });

                $(document).on('click', '.export', function () {
                    $('.tooltip:last').remove();
                });

                $(".ui-tooltip-content").parents('div').remove();
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {
                pageLoad();
            });


            // Reload grid code
            var RefreshGridInterval;
            var RefreshPeriod = 5; // Refresh every two minutes
            var ReloadPeriod = 0;

            $(window).load(function () {
                StartRefreshGridTimer();
            });


            function RefreshILMGrid() {
                // reset timeout warning to original minutes
                clearTimeout(RefreshGridInterval);
                RefreshGridInterval = setTimeout(RefreshILMGrid, RefreshPeriod * 60000);
                var grid = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM");
                SaveGridGroups(grid);

                // Refresh the grid
                $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderTop_RadAjaxManager1").ajaxRequest("");
            }

            function StartRefreshGridTimer() {
                RefreshGridInterval = setTimeout(RefreshILMGrid, RefreshPeriod * 60000);
            }

            function ResetRefreshGridTimer() {
                clearTimeout(RefreshGridInterval);
                StartRefreshGridTimer();
            }


            function SelectRow(index, custID) {
                var rgvILM = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM");
                rgvILM.get_masterTableView().get_dataItems()[index].set_selected("true");
                Set_Cookie("SelectedCustomerID", custID, expiry);
                Set_Cookie("SelectedRowIndex", index, expiry);

            }

            function ClearAllRows() {
                var masterTable = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM").get_masterTableView();
                masterTable.clearSelectedItems();
            }

            function ClientButtonClicking(sender, eventArgs) {
                var toolBar = sender;
                var button = eventArgs.get_item();
                var value = button.get_value();
                var btnText = button.get_text();

                if (value == "Reset") {
                    window.location.reload();
                }
                else if (value == "NewLead") {
                    var newLeadAccess = 1;
                    if (newLeadAccess == 2) {
                        url = 'https://www.car-research.com/WebXrm/NoAccessPage.aspx'
                    } else {
                        var url = 'https://www.car-research.com/carinteractive/';
                        url += 'internetleads_entry.asp?1=1&1=1&FromPage=ILM&program=vb&screen=srv&tabtitle=New Lead&WindowStyle=Hosted&xdb=CAR2&xDataEntry=T&xDealerId=1839&xEmpType=11&xSecurityLevel=47069&xString=823AAF3D-95B0-465D-B2B0-113B832EDBC4&xTimezone=1&xUserName=4677234&xOrigUserName=0';
                    }
                    
                    var wdw = window.open(url, "", params);
                }

                if (value == 'Filter') { // Toggle Selection
                    var filterstatus = ToggleLeftPane();
                    if (filterstatus == 0) {
                        button.set_text("<i class='fa fa-eye-slash fa-2x'></i> Hide Selection");
                    }
                    else {
                        button.set_text("<i class='fa fa-eye fa-2x'></i> Show Selection");
                    }
                }

                if (value == 'HideEmails') {
                    return true;
                }

                if (value == 'ShowEmails') {
                    return true;
                }

                if (value == 'ExpandAll') {
                    ExpandCollapseAllGroups(eventArgs, 0);
                    button.set_text("<i class='fa fa-compress fa-2x' ></i> Collapse All");
                    button.set_value('CollapseAll');
                    var hdnIsCollpased = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderTop_hdnIsCollpased');
                    hdnIsCollpased.value = 'False';
                }

                if (value == 'CollapseAll') {
                    ExpandCollapseAllGroups(eventArgs, 1);
                    button.set_text("<i class='fa fa-expand fa-2x' ></i> Expand All");
                    button.set_value('ExpandAll');
                    var hdnIsCollpased = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderTop_hdnIsCollpased');
                    hdnIsCollpased.value = 'True';
                }

                if (value == 'Pause') {
                    button.set_value('Resume');
                    button.set_text("<i class='fa fa-play fa-2x' ></i> Resume");
                    button.set_toolTip('Resume Automatic Refresh');
                    /*button.set_imageUrl('../Images/play_26.png');*/
                    clearTimeout(RefreshGridInterval);

                }

                if (value == 'Resume') {
                    button.set_value('Pause');
                    button.set_text("<i class='fa fa-pause fa-2x' ></i> Pause");
                    button.set_toolTip('Pause Automatic Refresh');
                    /*button.set_imageUrl('../Images/pause_26.png');*/
                    RefreshGridInterval = setTimeout(RefreshILMGrid, RefreshPeriod * 60000);
                }

                if (value == 'Refresh') {
                    var grid = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM")
                    SaveGridGroups(grid);
                }

                if (value != 'Refresh') {
                    CloseSlidingPane();
                    eventArgs.set_cancel(true);
                }

                return false;
            }

            function ExpandCollapseAllGroups(e, mode) { // 0 is for expand, 1 for collapse
                var grid = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM");
                var tableView = grid.get_masterTableView();
                var rows = tableView.get_element().rows;
                var followupOnlyMode = 'False';

                for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
                    var button = tableView._getGroupExpandButton(rows[i]);
                    if (button) {
                        var groupLevel = button.id.split("__")[2];

                        if ((groupLevel != 0) || (followupOnlyMode == 'True')) {
                            if (mode == 0 && button.className == "rgExpand")
                                tableView._toggleGroupsExpand(button, e);
                            else if (mode == 1 && button.className == "rgCollapse")
                                tableView._toggleGroupsExpand(button, e);

                        }
                    }
                }
            }


            function OpenCustomerPanel(url) {
                ToggleLeftPane(1);
                OpenSlidingPane();
                var frame = document.getElementById("iframeSlideOut");
                frame.src = url;

            }


            // Show/Hide Salesperson toolbar button
            function ToggleSalespersonToolbarButton(show, showBDC) {
                // 10/24/2012  Cng Ticket# 239083 showBDC show parameter for BDCRep
                var divSalesperson = document.getElementById("divSalesperson");
                var divBDCRep = document.getElementById("divBDCRep");
                if (show == 1) divSalesperson.style.display = ""; else divSalesperson.style.display = "none";
                if (showBDC == 1) divBDCRep.style.display = ""; else divBDCRep.style.display = "none";
            }

            function ShowFollowUpGrouping() {
                var divFollowupGrouping = document.getElementById("divFollowupGrouping");
                divFollowupGrouping.style.display = "";
            }

            function HideFollowUpGrouping() {
                var divFollowupGrouping = document.getElementById("divFollowupGrouping");
                divFollowupGrouping.style.display = "none";
            }

            function ShowScheduleTasksGrouping() {
                var divScheduledTaskGrouping = document.getElementById("divScheduledTaskGrouping");
                divScheduledTaskGrouping.style.display = "";
            }

            function HideScheduleTasksGrouping() {
                var divScheduledTaskGrouping = document.getElementById("divScheduledTaskGrouping");
                divScheduledTaskGrouping.style.display = "none";
            }

            function adjustSize() {


            }

            function ILM_GroupCollapsed(sender, eventArgs) {
                alert(eventArgs);
                alert(sender);
                var hdnGroupChanged = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderTop_hdnGroupChanged');
                hdnGroupChanged.value = 'True';
            }

            function ILM_GroupExpanded(sender, eventArgs) {
                var hdnGroupChanged = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderTop_hdnGroupChanged');
                hdnGroupChanged.value = 'True';
            }

        </script>
    


        <script type="text/javascript">
            // set the timeout period

            var timeoutPeriod = 19; // Default time out is 20 minutes

            // declare global variables to track the timeout and interval timers
            var timeoutWarning;

            function RefreshPage() {
                clearTimeout(timeoutWarning);

                // reset timeout warning to original minutes
                timeoutWarning = setTimeout(RefreshPage, timeoutPeriod * 60000);

                // create random number between 0 and 1000. Keep alive needs a random query string to work
                var decRound = Math.round(Math.random() * 1000);
                var imgRefresh = new Image(1, 1);

                // Call to keep alive refreshes the session
                imgRefresh.src = '../KeepAlive.aspx?id=' + decRound.toString();

            }

            //$('#overlay').show();

            function ClosePage() {
                // Close the page
                window.location = "../ClosePage.aspx?action=save";
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {
                $(".btn-slide").click(function () {
                    $("#slidePanel").slideToggle("slow");
                    $(this).toggleClass("active"); return false;
                });
            });

            function get_NewValue(sender, eventArgs) {
                if (eventArgs.get_newValue() == "") {
                    var phoneVal = sender;
                    phoneVal.clear();
                }
            }

<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">

    function ClientNodeClicking(sender, eventArgs) {
        var node = eventArgs.get_node();

        if (node.get_value() == "DateRangeParent" || node.get_value() == "DateRangeNode") { 
            // cancel post back for date range selection
            eventArgs.set_cancel(true);
        }
    }

    function onClientNodeToggle(sender, eventArgs) {
        var node = eventArgs.get_node();
        var i;
        var selectedNodes = "";

        for (i = 0; i < node.get_treeView().get_allNodes().length; i++) {
            if (node.get_treeView().get_allNodes()[i].get_expanded())
                selectedNodes += node.get_treeView().get_allNodes()[i].get_value() + "*";
        }

        Set_Cookie("ILMTree", selectedNodes, expiry);
    }
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            var today = new Date();
            var expiry = new Date(today.getTime() + 14 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);

            // Open sliding pane
            function OpenSlidingPane() {
                // Expand splitter
                var splitter = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSplitterMain");

            if (splitter) {
                var paneRight = splitter.getPaneById('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadPaneRight');
                var slidingZone = $find('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSlidingZoneRight');
                var paneCustomer = slidingZone.getPaneById('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSlidingPaneRight');

                // Set width to what Right Pane's width is at 80% of screen
                var width = paneRight.getContentElement().scrollWidth;

                // Show the right pane
                paneRight.expand();
                slidingZone.expandPane('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadPaneRight');
                slidingZone.expandPane('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSlidingPaneRight');
            }

            var frame = document.getElementById("iframeSlideOut");
            var frameDoc = frame.contentDocument || frame.contentWindow.document;
            if (frameDoc.documentElement) {
                frameDoc.removeChild(frameDoc.documentElement);
            }
            //frame.removeChild(frameDoc);
            frame.src = "javascript:false;";

            Set_Cookie("CustomerPaneOpen", "True", expiry);
            }

            // Adjust splitter height on load
            function SplitterLoaded(splitter, arg) {
                AdjustRightPaneSize();
            }

            function ClientBeforeResize(sender, Args) {
                alert('resize');
                Args.set_cancel(true);
            }

            function AdjustRightPaneSize() {
                var splitter = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSplitterMain");
            var slidingZone = $find('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSlidingZoneRight');
            var paneRight = splitter.getPaneById('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadPaneRight');
            var RadSlidingPaneRight = slidingZone.getPaneById('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSlidingPaneRight');

            // get the full window size, and adjust panel size
            var size = GetWindowSize();
            var width = (size[0] / 4) * 3; // 3/4th of screen
            var height = size[1] - 62; // account for toolbar and title height

            // if the window is small, then do not let panel width be more than 800px
            if (size[0] < 1000 && width > 800) width = 800;

            paneRight.set_height(height);
            RadSlidingPaneRight.set_height(height);
            // update panel width only if 2/3rd of screen is more than 800px
            RadSlidingPaneRight.set_width(width);

            // Hide Splitter's title bar
            var titleElement = RadSlidingPaneRight.getSlidingContainerTitle().parentNode.parentNode;
            titleElement.style.display = 'none';
            }

            var leftpanestatus = 0; // 0 is shown, 1 if hidden

            function ToggleLeftPane(action) { // Returns 0 is shown, 1 if hidden // action = 0 is open, action = 1 is close, action = null is toggle
                var splitter = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSplitterMain");

            if (splitter) {
                var pane = splitter.getPaneById("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadPaneLeft");

                if (action == null) {
                    if (pane.get_collapsed()) action = 0; else action = 1;
                    leftpanestatus = action;
                }

                if (action == 0)  // action == 0 => open
                    pane.expand();
                else
                    pane.collapse();
            }

            Set_Cookie("SelectionPaneOpen", !action, expiry);
            return action;
            }

            function CloseSlidingPane() {
                var splitter = $find("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSplitterMain");
            var slidingZone = $find('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSlidingZoneRight');

            var paneRight = splitter.getPaneById('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadPaneRight');

            // Collapse the right pane
            slidingZone.collapsePane("ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_RadSlidingPaneRight");
            paneRight.collapse();

            Set_Cookie("CustomerPaneOpen", "False", expiry);

            // return left pane to previous status
            ToggleLeftPane(leftpanestatus);
            }

            var SlideOutMaster = true;
        </script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function SetValue_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_xrmSalesPerson_hiddenEmployeeID(sender, eventArgs) {
   var item = eventArgs.get_item();
   var hiddenIDCtl = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_xrmSalesPerson_hiddenEmployeeID');
   if (hiddenIDCtl) hiddenIDCtl.value = item.get_value();
   hiddenTextCtl = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_xrmSalesPerson_hiddenEmployeeName');
   if (hiddenTextCtl) hiddenTextCtl.value = item.get_text();
}
function LoadFromHidden_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_xrmSalesPerson_hiddenEmployeeID() {
   var hiddenIDCtl = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_xrmSalesPerson_hiddenEmployeeID');
   var hiddenTextCtl = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_xrmSalesPerson_hiddenEmployeeName');
   var rcmbEmployee = $find('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_xrmSalesPerson_rcmbEmployee');
   if ((hiddenIDCtl.value != "") && (rcmbEmployee != null)) 
       rcmbEmployee.set_text(hiddenTextCtl.value);
}
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function showHideFilterItem_ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM() {
    var grid = $find('ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM');
    var filterid = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_ILMGridFilter_hdnshowhide');
    if (grid.get_masterTableView().get_isFilterItemVisible()) {  //if  INVISIBLE - then hide
        filterid.value = '0';
        grid.get_masterTableView().hideFilterItem(); 
        document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_ILMGridFilter_btnShowHideFilter').innerHTML = 'Show Filters';
        document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_ILMGridFilter_btnClearFilters').style.visibility = 'hidden';
    }
    else {
        filterid.value = '1';
        grid.get_masterTableView().showFilterItem();
        document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_ILMGridFilter_btnShowHideFilter').innerHTML = 'Hide Filters';
        document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_ILMGridFilter_btnClearFilters').style.visibility = 'visible';
    }
}
function clearFilters_ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM() {
    var filterid = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_ILMGridFilter_hdnshowhide');
    filterid.value = '1';
    var id ='ctl00_ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ContentPlaceHolderMiddlePane_rgvILM';
    clearFilters(id);
}
</script>
